Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. parts.append(\"\\n\".join(fm_lines))\n\n        # Output Contract section\n        oc_items = self.output_contract()\n        if oc_items:\n            oc_lines = [\"\", \"## Output Contract\"]\n            for item in oc_items:\n                oc_lines.append(f\"- {item}\")\n            parts.append(\"\\n\".join(oc_lines))\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(parts)\n\n    def build_retry(\n        self,\n        failure_reason: str,\n        remaining_placeholders: Optional[list[str]] = None,\n    ) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Build a retry prompt that includes the original prompt plus retry context.\"\"\"\n        base = self.build()\n        retry_parts = [base, \"\", \"## RETRY CONTEXT\", f\"Previous attempt failed: {failure_reason}\"]\n\n        if remaining_placeholders:\n            retry_parts.append(\"\")\n            retry_parts.append(\"The following placeholder sentinels MUST be resolved:\")\n            for ph in remaining_placeholders:\n                retry_parts.append(f\"  - {ph}\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(retry_parts)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# AnalyzeWorkflowPrompt\n# T02.09: run_with_timeout() — enforce step-level time budgets (NFR-001)\n   138→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   139→\n   140→\n   141→def run_with_timeout(fn: Callable[..., _T], timeout_s: float, *args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> _T:\n   142→    \"\"\"Run *fn* in a thread and raise TimeoutError if it exceeds *timeout_s* seconds.\n   143→\n   144→    Used to enforce:\n   145→      - SC-001: validate_and_configure() ≤ 30 s\n   146→      - SC-002: discover_components()     ≤ 60 s\n   147→\n   148→    Args:\n   149→        fn: Callable to execute.\n   150→        timeout_s: Maximum allowed wall-clock seconds.\n   151→        *args / **kwargs: Forwarded to *fn*.\n   152→\n   153→    Returns:\n   154→        The return value of *fn*.\n   155→\n   156→    Raises:\n   157→        TimeoutError: If *fn* does not complete within *timeout_s* seconds.\n   158→    \"\"\"\n   159→    with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as pool:\n   160→        future = pool.submit(fn, *args, **kwargs)\n   161→        try:\n   162→            return future.result(timeout=timeout_s)\n   163→        except concurrent.futures.TimeoutError:\n   164→            raise TimeoutError(\n   165→                f\"Operation timed out after {timeout_s}s\"\n   166→            )\n   167→\n   168→\n   169→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   170→# _determine_status()\n   171→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   172→\n   173→\n   174→def _determine_status(\n   175→    exit_code: int,\n   176→    timed_out: bool,\n   177→    stdout: str = \"\",\n   178→    artifact_path: Optional[Path] = None,\n   179→) -> PortifyStatus:\n   180→    \"\"\"Classify a step outcome from exit code, EXIT_RECOMMENDATION, and artifact.\n   181→\n   182→    Classification rules (priority order):\n   183→      1. exit 124 (or timed_out=True)  → TIMEOUT\n   184→      2. exit non-zero                 → ERROR\n   185→      3. exit 0 + marker + artifact    → PASS\n   186→      4. exit 0 + no marker + artifact → PASS_NO_SIGNAL  (triggers retry)\n   187→      5. exit 0 + artifact, no result  → PASS_NO_REPORT  (no retry)\n   188→      6. exit 0 + no artifact          → PASS_NO_REPORT\n   189→    \"\"\"\n   190→    if timed_out or exit_code == EXIT_CODE_TIMEOUT:\n   191→        return PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT\n   192→\n   193→    if exit_code != 0:\n   194→        return PortifyStatus.ERROR\n   195→\n   196→    # exit 0 paths\n   197→    has_marker = EXIT_RECOMMENDATION_MARKER in stdout\n   198→    artifact_exists = artifact_path is not None and Path(artifact_path).exists()\n   199→\n   200→    if has_marker and artifact_exists:\n   201→        return PortifyStatus.PASS\n   202→\n   203→    if not has_marker and artifact_exists:\n   204→        return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL  # triggers retry\n   205→\n   206→    # No artifact (or no result file) → no retry\n   207→    return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n   208→\n   209→\n   210→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   211→# Return contract helpers (T03.10)\n   212→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   213→\n   214→\n   215→def _build_resume_command(step_id: str, cli_name: str = \"portify\") -> str:\n   216→    \"\"\"Build the exact CLI command string for resuming from a step.\"\"\"\n   217→    return f\"superclaude cli-portify run --resume {step_id}\"\n   218→\n   219→\n   220→def _calculate_suggested_resume_budget(steps: list[PortifyStep]) -> int:\n   221→    \"\"\"Calculate suggested_resume_budget = remaining_steps_count * 25.\n   222→\n   223→    remaining = steps with PENDING or INCOMPLETE status.\n   224→    \"\"\"\n   225→    remaining = sum(\n   226→        1 for s in steps\n   227→        if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)\n   228→    )\n   229→    return remaining * 25\n   230→\n   231→\n   232→def _emit_return_contract(\n   233→    workdir: Path,\n   234→    outcome: PortifyOutcome,\n   235→    steps: list[PortifyStep],\n   241→    Returns the path to the emitted file.\n   242→    \"\"\"\n   243→    remaining_steps = [s.step_id for s in steps if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)]\n   244→ 265→\n   266→\n   267→class PortifyExecutor:\n   268→    \"\"\"Sequential pipeline executor for CLI Portify.\n   269→\n   270→    Usage:\n   271→        executor = PortifyExecutor(steps, workdir, step_runner\n   301→        self._interrupted: bool = False\n   302→        self._completed_steps: list[str] = []\n   303→        self._step_results: dict[str, PortifyStepResult] = {}\n   304→\n   305→        # Signal handler integration points (T03.04 / T03.09)\n   306→        self._prev_sigint: Optional[Callable] = None\n   307→        self._prev_sigterm: Optional[Callable] = None\n   308→\n   309→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   310→    # Signal handling (T03.09)\n   311→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   312→\n   313→    def _install_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n   314→        \"\"\"Register SIGINT / SIGTERM handlers for graceful shutdown.\"\"\"\n   315→        def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n   316→            self._interrupted = True\n   317→\n   318→        try:\n   319→            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n   320→            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n   321→        except (OSError, ValueError):\n   322→            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n   323→            pass\n   324→\n   325→    def _restore_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n   326→        \"\"\"Restore prior signal handlers after execution.\"\"\"\n   327→        try:\n   328→            if self._prev_sigint is not None:\n   329→                signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n   330→            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n   331→                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n   332→        except (OSError, ValueError):\n   333→            pass\n   334→\n   335→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   336→    # Step if this step should be executed given current mode.\"\"\"\n   341→        if self.dry_run:\n   342→            return step.phase_type in DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES\n   343→        return True\n   344→\n   345→    def _should_skip_for_resume(self, step: PortifyStep, resume_started: bool) -> bool:\n   346→        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be skipped because --resume hasn't reached it.\"\"\"\n   347→        return not resume_started\n   348→\n   349→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   350→    # Step execution\n   351→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   352→\n   353→    def _execute_step(self, step: PortifyStep) -> PortifyStatus:\n   354→        \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic (retry_limit=1 for PASS_NO_SIGNAL).\"\"\"\n   355→        if self._step_runner is not None:\n   356→            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n   357→        else:\n   358→            # Default: no-op (real subprocess invocation belongs in process.py)\n   359→            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n   360→\n   361→        artifact_path = step.output_file\n   362→        status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n   363→        self._ledger.consume(1)\n   364→\n   365→        # Retry once on PASS_NO_SIGNAL (retry_limit=1 per NFR-002)\n   366→        if status == PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL and step.retry_limit >= 1:\n   367→            if self._ledger.can_launch():\n   368→                if self._step_runner is not None:\n   369→                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n   370→                else:\n   371→                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n   372→                self._ledger.consume(1)\n   373→                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n   374→\n   375→        return status\n   376→\n   377→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   378→    # Main execution loop\n   379→    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n   380→\n   381→    def run(self) -> PortifyOutcome:\n   382→        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n   383→        self._install_signal_handlers()\n   384→        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n   385→        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n   386→\n   387→        try:\n   388→            for step in self.steps:\n   389→                # Resume skip logic\n   395→                if not resume_started:\n   396→                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n   397→                        resume_started = True\n   398→                    else:\n   399→                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n   400→                        continue\n   401→\n   402→                # Dry-run filtering\n   403→                if not self._should_execute(step):\n   404→                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n   405→                    continue\n   406→\n   407→                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n   408→                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n   409→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n   410→                    break\n   411→\n   412→                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n   413→                status = self._execute_step(step)\n   414→                step.status = status\n   415→\n   416→                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n   417→                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n   418→                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n   419→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n   420→                    break\n   421→                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n   422→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n   423→                    break\n   424→\n   425→                # Check interrupt after step completes\n   426→                if self._interrupted:\n   427→                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n   428→                    break\n   429→\n   430→        finally:\n   431→            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n   432→            # PortifyStepResult,\n    PortifyValidationError,\n    TurnLedger,\n)\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Constants\n#  \"prompts-executor-design\": {\n        \"step_id\": \"prompts-executor-design\",\n        \"phase_type\": PortifyPhaseType.SPECIFICATION,\n        \"timeout_s\": 600,\n        \"retry_limit\": 1,\n    },\n    \"pipeline-spec-assembly\": {\n        \"step_id\": \"pipeline-spec-assembly\",\n        \"phase_type\": PortifyPhaseType.SPECIFICATION,\n        \"timeout_s\": 600,\n \"retry_limit\": 0,\n    },\n}\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T02.09: run_with_timeout() — enforce step-level time budgets (NFR-001)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_with_timeout(fn: Callable[..., _T], timeout_s: float, *args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> _T:\n    \"\"\"Run *fn* in a thread and raise TimeoutError if it exceeds *timeout_s* seconds.\n\n    Used to enforce:\n      - SC-001: validate_and_configure() ≤ 30 s\n      - SC-002: discover_components()     ≤ 60 s\n\n    Args:\n        fn: Callable to execute.\n        timeout_s: Maximum allowed wall-clock seconds.\n        *args / **kwargs: Forwarded to *fn*.\n\n    Returns:\n        The return value of *fn*.\n\n    Raises:\n        TimeoutError: If *fn* does not complete within *timeout_s* seconds.\n    \"\"\"\n    with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=1) as pool:\n        future = pool.submit(fn, *args, **kwargs)\n        try:\n            return future.result(timeout=timeout_s)\n        except concurrent.futures.TimeoutError:\n            raise TimeoutError(\n                f\"Operation timed out after {timeout_s}s\"\n            )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# _determine_status()\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _determine_status(\n    exit_code: int,\n    timed_out: bool,\n    stdout: str = \"\",\n    artifact_path: Optional[Path] = None,\n) -> PortifyStatus:\n    \"\"\"Classify a step outcome from exit code, EXIT_RECOMMENDATION, and artifact.\n\n    Classification rules (priority order):\n      1. exit 124 (or timed_out=True)  → TIMEOUT\n      2. exit non-zero                 → ERROR\n      3. exit 0 + marker + artifact    → PASS\n      4. exit 0 + no marker + artifact → PASS_NO_SIGNAL  (triggers retry)\n      5. exit 0 + artifact, no result  → PASS_NO_REPORT  (no retry)\n      6. exit 0 + no artifact          → PASS_NO_REPORT\n    \"\"\"\n    if timed_out or exit_code == EXIT_CODE_TIMEOUT:\n        return PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return PortifyStatus.ERROR\n\n    # exit 0 paths\n    has_marker = EXIT_RECOMMENDATION_MARKER in stdout\n    artifact_exists = artifact_path is not None and Path(artifact_path).exists()\n\n    if has_marker and artifact_exists:\n        return PortifyStatus.PASS\n\n    if not has_marker and artifact_exists:\n        return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL  # triggers retry\n\n    # No artifact (or no result file) → no retry\n    return PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Return contract helpers (T03.10)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _build_resume_command(step_id: str, cli_name: str = \"portify\") -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build the exact CLI command string for resuming from a step.\"\"\"\n    return f\"superclaude cli-portify run --resume {step_id}\"\n\n\ndef _calculate_suggested_resume_budget(steps: list[PortifyStep]) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Calculate suggested_resume_budget = remaining_steps_count * 25.\n\n    remaining = steps with PENDING or INCOMPLETE status.\n    \"\"\"\n    remaining = sum(\n        1 for s in steps\n        if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)\n    )\n    return remaining * 25\n\n\ndef _emit_return_contract(\n    workdir: Path,\n    outcome: PortifyOutcome,\n    steps: list[PortifyStep],\n    completed_steps: list[str],\n    resume_from_step_id: str = \"\",\n) -> Path:\n    \"\"\"Emit return-contract.yaml to the workdir on ALL outcome paths (SC-011).\n\n    Returns the path to the emitted file.\n    \"\"\"\n    remaining_steps = [s.step_id for s in steps if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE)]\n    resume_command = _build_resume_command(resume_from_step_id) if resume_from_step_id else \"\"\n    suggested_budget = _calculate_suggested_resume_budget(steps)\n\n    contract = {\n        \"outcome\": outcome.value,\n        \"completed_steps\": completed_steps,\n        \"remaining_steps\": remaining_steps,\n        \"resume_command\": resume_command,\n        \"suggested_resume_budget\": suggested_budget,\n    }\n\n    workdir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    contract_path = workdir / \"return-contract.yaml\"\n    with open(contract_path, \"w\") as fh:\n        yaml.safe_dump(contract, fh, default_flow_style=False)\n    return contract_path\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# PortifyExecutor\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass PortifyExecutor:\n    \"\"\"Sequential pipeline executor for CLI Portify.\n\n    Usage:\n        executor = PortifyExecutor(steps, workdir, dry_run=False)\n        outcome = executor.run()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        steps: list[PortifyStep],\n        workdir: Path,\n        *,\n        dry_run: bool = False,\n        resume_from: str = \"\",\n        turn_budget: int = 200,\n        step_runner: Optional[Callable[[PortifyStep], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"\n        Args:\n            steps: Ordered list of steps in registered order.\n            workdir: Working directory for artifacts and return contract.\n            dry_run: If True, filter execution to DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES only.\n            resume_from: Step ID to resume from (skip all prior steps).\n            turn_budget: Total Claude-invocation budget (TurnLedger).\n            step_runner: Optional callable (step) -> (exit_code, stdout, timed_out).\n                         Used for testing; real runs use subprocess.\n        \"\"\"\n        self.steps = steps\n        self.workdir = workdir\n        self.dry_run = dry_run\n        self.resume_from = resume_from\n        self._ledger = TurnLedger(total_budget=turn_budget)\n        self._step_runner = step_runner\n        self._interrupted: bool = False\n        self._completed_steps: list[str] = []\n        self._step_results: dict[str, PortifyStepResult] = {}\n\n        # Signal handler integration points (T03.04 / T03.09)\n        self._prev_sigint: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._prev_sigterm: Optional[Callable] = None\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Signal handling (T03.09)\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _install_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Register SIGINT / SIGTERM handlers for graceful shutdown.\"\"\"\n        def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n            self._interrupted = True\n\n        try:\n            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n            pass\n\n    def _restore_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Restore prior signal handlers after execution.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if self._prev_sigint is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            pass\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step filtering\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _should_execute(self, step: PortifyStep) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be executed given current mode.\"\"\"\n        if self.dry_run:\n            return step.phase_type in DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES\n        return True\n\n    def _should_skip_for_resume(self, step: PortifyStep, resume_started: bool) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be skipped because --resume hasn't reached it.\"\"\"\n        return not resume_started\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step execution\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _execute_step(self, step: PortifyStep) -> PortifyStatus:\n        \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic (retry_limit=1 for PASS_NO_SIGNAL).\"\"\"\n        if self._step_runner is not None:\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n        else:\n            # Default: no-op (real subprocess invocation belongs in process.py)\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n\n        artifact_path = step.output_file\n        status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n        self._ledger.consume(1)\n\n        # Retry once on PASS_NO_SIGNAL (retry_limit=1 per NFR-002)\n        if status == PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL and step.retry_limit >= 1:\n            if self._ledger.can_launch():\n                if self._step_runner is not None:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n                else:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n                self._ledger.consume(1)\n                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n\n        return status\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Main execution loop\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def run(self) -> PortifyOutcome:\n        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n        self._install_signal_handlers()\n        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n\n        try:\n            for step in self.steps:\n                # Check for interrupt before each step\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Resume skip logic\n                if not resume_started:\n                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n                        resume_started = True\n                    else:\n                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                        continue\n\n                # Dry-run filtering\n                if not self._should_execute(step):\n                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                    continue\n\n                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n                    break\n\n                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n                status = self._execute_step(step)\n                step.status = status\n\n                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n                    break\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n                    break\n\n                # Check interrupt after step completes\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n        finally:\n            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n            # Determine resume step (first non-completed step)\n            resume_step = \"\"\n            for s in self.steps:\n                if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE):\n                    resume_step = s.step_id\n                    break\n            _emit_return_contract(\n                workdir=self.workdir,\n                outcome=outcome if not self.dry_run else PortifyOutcome.DRY_RUN,\n                steps=self.steps,\n                completed_steps=self._completed_steps,\n                resume_from_step_id=resume_step,\n            )\n\n        return outcome\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Phase 5 Step Execution Functions (T05.01, T05.02, T05.04)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef execute_protocol_mapping_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    inventory: list,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the protocol-mapping step (T05.01, FR-013, FR-014).\n\n    Runs Claude via subprocess to produce ``workdir/protocol-map.md`` with\n    required YAML frontmatter and EXIT_RECOMMENDATION marker.  Applies G-002\n    gate after execution; retries once on PASS_NO_SIGNAL.\n\n    Args:\n        config_cli_name: CLI name being portified.\n        inventory: List of ComponentEntry objects.\n        workdir: Working directory where protocol-map.md will be written.\n        process_runner: Optional callable (prompt, output_path) -> (exit_code, stdout, timed_out).\n                        Used for testing; prompts_executor_content: str,\n) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Programmatically concatenate and deduplicate 3 input specs (T06.04, FR-023, SC-005).\n\n    Concatenates the three spec artifacts with section Prompts and Executor Design\\n\\n\" + prompts_executor_content.strip())\n\n    assembled = \"\\n\\n\".join(sections)\n\n    # Deduplicate repeated YAML frontmatter blocks (keep only first occurrence).\n    # A frontmatter block starts at the beginning of a line with exactly \"---\"\n    # followed by key: value lines and closed by another \"---\" line.\n    import re as _re\n    frontmatter_pattern = _re.compile(r\"^---\\n(?:[^\\n]+\\n)*?---\\n\", _re.MULTILINE)\n    matches = list(frontmatter_pattern.finditer(assembled))\n    if len(matches) > 1:\n        # Remove all but ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass BasePromptBuilder:\n    \"\"\"Base class for all CLI Portify prompt builders.\n\n    Subclasses must implement:\n    - step_name: str\n    - _body() -> str  (main prompt body)\n    - required_frontmatter() -> list[str]\n    - output_contract() -> list[str]\n    - input_artifacts() -> list[Path]\n    \"\"\"\n\n    step_name: str = \"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, ctx: PromptContext) -> None:\n        self.ctx = ctx\n\n    def input_artifacts(self) -> list[Path]:\n        \"\"\"Return list of prior-step artifact Paths referenced by this prompt.\"\"\"\n        return []\n\n    def required_frontmatter(self) -> list[str]:\n        \"\"\"Return list of required YAML frontmatter field names.\"\"\"\n        return []\n\n    def output_contract(self) -> list[str]:\n        \"\"\"Return list of output contract requirements.\"\"\"\n        return []\n\n    def _body(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Return the main prompt body text.\"\"\"\n        return \"\"\n\n    def build(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Build the full prompt string with @path references, output contract, and frontmatter.\"\"\"\n        parts: list[str] = []\n\n        # @path references for prior artifacts\n        for artifact in self.input_artifacts():\n            parts.append(f\"@{artifact.resolve()}\")\n\n        # Main body\n        body = self._body()\n        if body:\n            parts.append(body)\n\n        # Required Frontmatter section\n        fm_fields = self.required_frontmatter()\n        if fm_fields:\n            fm_lines = [\"\", \"## Required Frontmatter\", \"```yaml\", \"---\"]\n            for f in fm_fields:\n                fm_lines.append(f\"{f}: <value>\")\n            fm_lines += [\"---\", \"```\"]\n            parts.append(\"\\n\".join(fm_lines))\n\n        # Output Contract section\n        oc_items = self.output_contract()\n        if oc_items:\n            oc_lines = [\"\", \"## Output Contract\"]\n            for item in oc_items:\n                oc_lines.append(f\"- {item}\")\n            parts.append(\"\\n\".join(oc_lines))\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(parts)\n\n    def build_retry(\n        self,\n        failure_reason: str,\n        remaining_placeholders: Optional[list[str]] = None,\n    ) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Build a retry prompt that includes the original prompt plus retry context.\"\"\"\n        base = self.build()\n        retry_parts = [base, \"\", \"## RETRY CONTEXT\", f\"Previous attempt failed: {failure_reason}\"]\n\n        if remaining_placeholders:\n            retry_parts.append(\"\")\n            retry_parts.append(\"The following placeholder sentinels MUST be resolved:\")\n            for ph in remaining_placeholders:\n                retry_parts.append(f\"  - {ph}\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(retry_parts)\n\n\n#      def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n            self._interrupted = True\n\n        try:\n            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n            pass\n\n    def signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n        except (OSError, PortifyStep) -> PortifyStatus:\n        \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic (retry_limit=1 for PASS_NO_SIGNAL).\"\"\"\n        if self._step_runner is not None:\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n        else:\n            # Default: no-op (real subprocess invocation belongs in process.py)\n            exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n\n        artifact_path = step.output_file\n        status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n        self._ledger.consume(1)\n\n        # Retry once on PASS_NO_SIGNAL (retry_limit=1 per NFR-002)\n        if status == PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL and step.retry_limit >= 1:\n            if self._ledger.can_launch():\n                if self._step_runner is not None:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n                else:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n                self._ledger.consume(1)\n                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n\n        return status\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Main execution loop\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def run(self) -> PortifyOutcome:\n        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n        self._install_signal_handlers()\n        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n\n        try:\n            for step in self.steps:\n                # Check for interrupt before each step\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Resume skip logic\n                if not resume_started:\n                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n                        resume_started = True\n                    else:\n                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                        continue\n\n                # Dry-run filtering\n                if not self._should_execute(step):\n                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                    continue\n\n                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n                    break\n\n                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n                status = self._execute_step(step)\n                step.status = status\n\n                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n                    break\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n                    break\n\n                # Check interrupt after step completes\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n        finally:\n            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n            # Determine resume step (first non-completed step)\n            resume_step = \"\"\n            for s in self.steps:\n                if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE):\n                    resume_step = s.step_id\n                    break\n            _emit_return_contract(\n                workdir=self.workdir,\n                outcome=outcome if not self.dry_run else PortifyOutcome.DRY_RUN,\n                steps=self.steps,\n                completed_steps=self._completed_steps,\n                resume_from_step_id=resume_step,\n            )\n\n        return outcome\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Phase 5 Step Execution Functions (T05.01, T05.02, T05.04)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef execute_protocol_mapping_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    inventory: list,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the protocol-mapping step (T05.01, FR-013, FR-014).\n\n    Runs Claude via subprocess to produce ``workdir/protocol-map.md`` with\n    required YAML frontmatter and EXIT_RECOMMENDATION marker. prompts_executor_content: str,\n) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Programmatically concatenate and deduplicate 3 input specs (T06.04, FR-023, SC-005).\n\n    Concatenates the three spec artifacts with section headers, then deduplicates\n    repeated YAML frontmatter sections before passing to Claude synthesis.\n\n    Args:\n        step_graph_content: Content of step-graph-spec.md.\n        models_gates_content: Content of models-gates-spec.md.\n        prompts_executor_content: Content of prompts-executor-spec.md.\n\n    Returns:\n        Assembled and deduplicated content string ready for Claude synthesis.\n    \"\"\"\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    if step_graph_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Step Graph Design\\n\\n\" + step_graph_content.strip())\n\n    if models_gates_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Models and Gates Design\\n\\n\" + models_gates_content.strip())\n\n    if prompts_executor_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Prompts and Executor Design\\n\\n\" + prompts_executor_content.strip())\n\n    assembled = \"\\n\\n\".join(sections)\n\n    # Deduplicate repeated YAML frontmatter blocks (keep only first occurrence).\n    # A frontmatter block starts at the beginning of a line with exactly \"---\"\n    # followed by key: value lines and closed by another \"---\" line.\n    import re as _re\n    frontmatter_pattern = _re.compile(r\"^---\\n(?:[^\\n]+\\n)*?---\\n\", _re.MULTILINE)\n    matches = list(frontmatter_pattern.finditer(assembled))\n    if len(matches) > 1:\n        # Remove all but the first frontmatter block (reverse order to preserve offsets)\n        for match in reversed(matches[1:]):\n            assembled = assembled[:match.start()] + assembled[match.end():]\n\n    return assembled\n\n\ndef execute_pipeline_spec_assembly_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        steps: list[PortifyStep],\n        workdir: Path,\n        *,\n        dry_run: bool = False,\n        resume_from: str = \"\",\n ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _install_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Register SIGINT / SIGTERM handlers for graceful shutdown.\"\"\"\n        def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n            self._interrupted = True\n\n        try:\n            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n            pass\n\n    def _restore_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Restore prior signal handlers after execution.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if self._prev_sigint is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            pass\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step filtering\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _should_execute(self, step: PortifyStep) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be executed given current mode.\"\"\"\n        if self.dry_run:\n            return step.phase_type in DRY_RUN_PHASE_TYPES\n        return True\n\n    def _should_skip_for_resume(self, step: PortifyStep, resume_started: bool) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be skipped because --resume hasn't reached it.\"\"\"\n        return not resume_started\n\n    # PASS_NO_SIGNAL (retry_limit=1 per NFR-002)\n        if status == PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL and step.retry_limit >= 1:\n            if self._ledger.can_launch():\n                if self._step_runner is not None:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n                else:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n                self._ledger.consume(1)\n                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n\n        return status\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Main execution loop\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def run(self) -> PortifyOutcome:\n        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n        self._install_signal_handlers()\n        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n\n        try:\n            for step in self.steps:\n                # Check for interrupt before each step\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Resume skip logic\n                if not resume_started:\n                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n                        resume_started = True\n                    else:\n                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                        continue\n\n                # Dry-run filtering\n                if not self._should_execute(step):\n                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                    continue\n\n                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n                    break\n\n                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n                status = self._execute_step(step)\n                step.status = status\n\n                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n                    break\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n                    break\n\n                # Check interrupt after step completes\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n        finally:\n            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n            # Determine resume step (first non-completed step)\n            resume_step = \"\"\n            for s in self.steps:\n                if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE):\n                    resume_step = s.step_id\n                    break\n            _emit_return_contract(\n                workdir=self.workdir,\n                outcome=outcome if not self.dry_run else PortifyOutcome.DRY_RUN,\n                steps=self.steps,\n                completed_steps=self._completed_steps,\n                resume_from_step_id=resume_step,\n            )\n\n        return outcome\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Phase 5 Step Execution Functions (T05.01, T05.02, T05.04)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef execute_protocol_mapping_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    inventory: list,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the protocol-mapping step (T05.01, FR-013, FR-014).\n\n    Runs Claude via subprocess to produce ``workdir/protocol-map.md`` with\n    required YAML frontmatter and EXIT_RECOMMENDATION marker. prompts_executor_content: str,\n) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Programmatically concatenate and deduplicate 3 input specs (T06.04, FR-023, SC-005).\n\n    Concatenates the three spec artifacts with section headers, then deduplicates\n    repeated YAML frontmatter sections before passing to Claude synthesis.\n\n    Args:\n        step_graph_content: Content of step-graph-spec.md.\n        models_gates_content: Content of models-gates-spec.md.\n        prompts_executor_content: Content of prompts-executor-spec.md.\n\n    Returns:\n        Assembled and deduplicated content string ready for Claude synthesis.\n    \"\"\"\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    if step_graph_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Step Graph Design\\n\\n\" + step_graph_content.strip())\n\n    if models_gates_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Models and Gates Design\\n\\n\" + models_gates_content.strip())\n\n    if prompts_executor_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Prompts and Executor Design\\n\\n\" + prompts_executor_content.strip())\n\n    assembled = \"\\n\\n\".join(sections)\n\n    # Deduplicate repeated YAML frontmatter blocks (keep only first occurrence).\n    # A frontmatter block starts at the beginning of a line with exactly \"---\"\n    # followed by key: value lines and closed by another \"---\" line.\n    import re as _re\n    frontmatter_pattern = _re.compile(r\"^---\\n(?:[^\\n]+\\n)*?---\\n\", _re.MULTILINE)\n    matches = list(frontmatter_pattern.finditer(assembled))\n    if len(matches) > 1:\n        # Remove all but the first frontmatter block (reverse order to preserve offsets)\n        for match in reversed(matches[1:]):\n            assembled = assembled[:match.start()] + assembled[match.end():]\n\n    return assembled\n\n\ndef execute_pipeline_spec_assembly_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> a thread and raise TimeoutError if it exceeds *timeout_s* seconds.\n\n    Used to enforce:\n      - SC-001: validate_and_configure() ≤ 30 s\n      - SC-002: discover_components()     ≤ 60 s\n\n ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _install_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Register SIGINT / SIGTERM handlers for graceful shutdown.\"\"\"\n        def _handle(signum: int, frame) -> None:\n            self._interrupted = True\n\n        try:\n            self._prev_sigint = signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, _handle)\n            self._prev_sigterm = signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, _handle)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            # Non-main thread or OS doesn't support — skip gracefully\n            pass\n\n    def _restore_signal_handlers(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Restore prior signal handlers after execution.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            if self._prev_sigint is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._prev_sigint)\n            if self._prev_sigterm is not None:\n                signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._prev_sigterm)\n        except (OSError, ValueError):\n            pass\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Step filtering\n    # -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Return True if this step should be skipped because --resume hasn't reached it.\"\"\"\n        return not resume_started\n\n    # self._step_runner is not None:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = self._step_runner(step)\n                else:\n                    exit_code, stdout, timed_out = 0, \"\", False\n                self._ledger.consume(1)\n                status = _determine_status(exit_code, timed_out, stdout, artifact_path)\n\n        return status\n\n    # PortifyOutcome:\n        \"\"\"Execute all steps sequentially. Returns pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n        self._install_signal_handlers()\n        outcome = PortifyOutcome.SUCCESS\n        resume_started = (self.resume_from == \"\")  # True if no resume target\n\n        try:\n            for step in self.steps:\n                # Check for interrupt before each step\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n                # Resume skip logic\n                if not resume_started:\n                    if step.step_id == self.resume_from:\n                        resume_started = True\n                    else:\n                        step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                        continue\n\n                # Dry-run filtering\n                if not self._should_execute(step):\n                    step.status = PortifyStatus.SKIPPED\n                    continue\n\n                # Budget check before launch (FR-040)\n                if not self._ledger.can_launch():\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.HALTED\n                    break\n\n                step.status = PortifyStatus.RUNNING\n                status = self._execute_step(step)\n                step.status = status\n\n                if status in (PortifyStatus.PASS, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, PortifyStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                    self._completed_steps.append(step.step_id)\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.TIMEOUT:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.TIMEOUT\n                    break\n                elif status == PortifyStatus.ERROR:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.FAILURE\n                    break\n\n                # Check interrupt after step completes\n                if self._interrupted:\n                    outcome = PortifyOutcome.INTERRUPTED\n                    break\n\n        finally:\n            self._restore_signal_handlers()\n            # Determine resume step (first non-completed step)\n            resume_step = \"\"\n            for s in self.steps:\n                if s.status in (PortifyStatus.PENDING, PortifyStatus.INCOMPLETE):\n                    resume_step = s.step_id\n                    break\n            _emit_return_contract(\n                workdir=self.workdir,\n                outcome=outcome if not self.dry_run else PortifyOutcome.DRY_RUN,\n                steps=self.steps,\n                completed_steps=self._completed_steps,\n                resume_from_step_id=resume_step,\n            )\n\n        return outcome\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Phase 5 Step Execution Functions (T05.01, T05.02, T05.04)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef execute_protocol_mapping_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    inventory: list,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> PortifyStepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute the protocol-mapping step (T05.01, FR-013, FR-014).\n\n    Runs Claude via subprocess to produce ``workdir/protocol-map.md`` with\n    required YAML frontmatter and EXIT_RECOMMENDATION marker. prompts_executor_content: str,\n) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Programmatically concatenate and deduplicate 3 input specs (T06.04, FR-023, SC-005).\n\n    Concatenates the three spec artifacts with section headers, then deduplicates\n    repeated YAML frontmatter sections before passing to Claude synthesis.\n\n    Args:\n        step_graph_content: Content of step-graph-spec.md.\n        models_gates_content: Content of models-gates-spec.md.\n        prompts_executor_content: Content of prompts-executor-spec.md.\n\n    Returns:\n        Assembled and deduplicated content string ready for Claude synthesis.\n    \"\"\"\n    sections: list[str] = []\n\n    if step_graph_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Step Graph Design\\n\\n\" + step_graph_content.strip())\n\n    if models_gates_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Models and Gates Design\\n\\n\" + models_gates_content.strip())\n\n    if prompts_executor_content.strip():\n        sections.append(\"## Prompts and Executor Design\\n\\n\" + prompts_executor_content.strip())\n\n    assembled = \"\\n\\n\".join(sections)\n\n    # Deduplicate repeated YAML frontmatter blocks (keep only first occurrence).\n    # A frontmatter block starts at the beginning of a line with exactly \"---\"\n    # followed by key: value lines and closed by another \"---\" line.\n    import re as _re\n    frontmatter_pattern = _re.compile(r\"^---\\n(?:[^\\n]+\\n)*?---\\n\", _re.MULTILINE)\n    matches = list(frontmatter_pattern.finditer(assembled))\n    if len(matches) > 1:\n        # Remove all but the first frontmatter block (reverse order to preserve offsets)\n        for match in reversed(matches[1:]):\n            assembled = assembled[:match.start()] + assembled[match.end():]\n\n    return assembled\n\n\ndef execute_pipeline_spec_assembly_step(\n    config_cli_name: str,\n    workdir: Path,\n    process_runner: Optional[Callable[[str, Path], tuple[int, str, bool]]] = None,\n) -> Exits cleanly with code 0.\n\n    Args:\n        config_cli_name: CLI name being portified (used in instructions).\n        workdir: Working directory where phase2-approval.yaml will be written.\n        step_results: List of PortifyStepResult objects from Phase 2 steps.\n                      If None, skips gate-pass validation.\n        _exit: If True (default), calls sys.exit(0). Set False in tests.\n\n    Raises:\n        PortifyValidationError: If blocking gates have not passed or portify-spec.md\n                                is missing or has an empty step_mapping section.\n    \"\"\"\n    #
